You can exchange files with other applications in many different formats.\r\n\r\nKrita is being developed by an international community of open source enthusiasts who want to make a great digital painting application available as widely as possible.\r\n\r\nIf you buy Krita in the Windows store, you will support the development of Krita directly: currently, two volunteers from the Krita community are sponsored to work full-time on Krita.
